SELECT [m].[Id], [m].[Name], [m].[Url], [t].[SubmenuId], [t].[SubmenuName], [t].[Url], [t].[Id]
FROM [Menu] AS [m]
OUTER APPLY (
    SELECT [m0].[Id] AS [SubmenuId], COALESCE([m0].[Name], N'') AS [SubmenuName], (
        SELECT TOP(1) [m1].[Url]
        FROM [Menu] AS [m1]
        WHERE [m1].[Id] = [m0].[Id]) AS [Url], [r].[Id]
    FROM [RoleMenuPermission] AS [r]
    INNER JOIN [Menu] AS [m0] ON [r].[SubMenuId] = [m0].[Id]
    WHERE [r].[RoleId] = @__roleId_0 AND [m].[Id] = [r].[MenuId]
) AS [t]
WHERE [m].[ParentId] = N'0'
ORDER BY [m].[Id], [t].[Id]

SELECT [m].[Id], [m].[Name], [m].[Url], [t].[SubmenuId], [t].[SubmenuName], [t].[Url], [t].[Id]
FROM [Menu] AS [m]
OUTER APPLY (
    SELECT [m0].[Id] AS [SubmenuId], COALESCE([m0].[Name], N'') AS [SubmenuName], (
        SELECT TOP(1) [m1].[Url]
        FROM [Menu] AS [m1]
        WHERE [m1].[Id] = [m0].[Id]) AS [Url], [r].[Id]
    FROM [RoleMenuPermission] AS [r]
    INNER JOIN [Menu] AS [m0] ON [r].[SubMenuId] = [m0].[Id]
    WHERE [r].[RoleId] = @__roleId_0 AND [m].[Id] = [r].[MenuId]
) AS [t]
WHERE [m].[ParentId] = N'0'
ORDER BY [m].[Id], [t].[Id]

FROM [Menu] AS [m]
OUTER APPLY (
    SELECT [m0].[Id] AS [SubmenuId], COALESCE([m0].[Name], N'') AS [SubmenuName], (

SELECT [m].[Id], [m].[Name], [m].[Url], [t].[SubmenuId], [t].[SubmenuName], [t].[Url], [t].[Id]
FROM [Menu] AS [m]
OUTER APPLY (
    SELECT [m0].[Id] AS [SubmenuId], COALESCE([m0].[Name], N'') AS [SubmenuName], (
        SELECT TOP(1) [m1].[Url]
        FROM [Menu] AS [m1]
        WHERE [m1].[Id] = [m0].[Id]) AS [Url], [r].[Id]
    FROM [RoleMenuPermission] AS [r]
    INNER JOIN [Menu] AS [m0] ON [r].[SubMenuId] = [m0].[Id]
    WHERE [r].[RoleId] = @__roleId_0 AND [m].[Id] = [r].[MenuId]
) AS [t]
WHERE [m].[ParentId] = N'0'
ORDER BY [m].[Id], [t].[Id]

SELECT [m].[Id], [m].[Name], [m].[Url], [t].[SubmenuId], [t].[SubmenuName], [t].[Url], [t].[Id]
FROM [Menu] AS [m]
OUTER APPLY (
    SELECT [m0].[Id] AS [SubmenuId], COALESCE([m0].[Name], N'') AS [SubmenuName], (
        SELECT TOP(1) [m1].[Url]
        FROM [Menu] AS [m1]
        WHERE [m1].[Id] = [m0].[Id]) AS [Url], [r].[Id]
    FROM [RoleMenuPermission] AS [r]
    INNER JOIN [Menu] AS [m0] ON [r].[SubMenuId] = [m0].[Id]
    WHERE [r].[RoleId] = @__roleId_0 AND [m].[Id] = [r].[MenuId]

FROM [Menu] AS [m]
OUTER APPLY (
    SELECT [m0].[Id] AS [SubmenuId], COALESCE([m0].[Name], N'') AS [SubmenuName], (
        SELECT TOP(1) [m1].[Url]
        FROM [Menu] AS [m1]
